### [73] [MRD: Multi-resolution Retrieval-Detection Fusion for High-Resolution Image Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02906)
*Fan Yang,Kaihao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MRD提出了一种无需训练的多分辨率检索-检测融合框架，通过多分辨率语义融合解决高分辨率图像理解中目标对象被分割到不同图像块导致的语义相似性偏差问题，并结合开放词汇目标检测实现全局尺度目标定位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高分辨率图像对多模态大语言模型仍是一个重大挑战。现有方法通过将图像分割成小块并计算每个块与查询的语义相似度来选择相关区域，但这种方法会将完整对象分割到多个图像块中，破坏语义相似度计算，导致语义相似性偏差。

Method: 提出MRD框架：1）多分辨率语义融合方法，整合不同分辨率下获得的语义相似度图，产生更准确的语义信息并保持目标对象完整性；2）引入开放词汇目标检测模型，通过滑动窗口方法识别对象区域，实现全局尺度的直接目标定位。

Result: 在不同MLLMs上进行的高分辨率图像理解基准测试实验证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: MRD框架通过多分辨率检索-检测融合，有效解决了高分辨率图像理解中目标对象分割导致的语义相似性偏差问题，实现了更准确的目标定位和图像理解。

Abstract: Understanding high-resolution images remains a significant challenge for multimodal large language models (MLLMs). Recent study address this issue by dividing the image into smaller crops and computing the semantic similarity between each crop and a query using a pretrained retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) model. The most relevant crops are then selected to localize the target object and suppress irrelevant information. However, such crop-based processing can fragment complete objects across multiple crops, thereby disrupting the computation of semantic similarity. In our experiments, we find that image crops of objects with different sizes are better handled at different resolutions. Based on this observation, we propose Multi-resolution Retrieval-Detection (MRD), a training-free framework for high-resolution image understanding. To address the issue of semantic similarity bias caused by objects being split across different image crops, we propose a multi-resolution semantic fusion method, which integrates semantic similarity maps obtained at different resolutions to produce more accurate semantic information and preserve the integrity of target objects. Furthermore, to achieve direct localization of target objects at a global scale, we introduce an open-vocalbulary object detection (OVD) model that identifies object regions using a sliding-window approach.Experiments on high-resolution image understanding benchmarks using different MLLMs demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach.

中文标题: MRD：用于高分辨率图像理解的多分辨率检索-检测融合

中文摘要: 理解高分辨率图像对多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）仍然是一个重大挑战。最近的研究通过将图像分割成较小的图像块，并使用预训练的检索增强生成（RAG）模型计算每个图像块与查询的语义相似度来解决这个问题。然后选择最相关的图像块来定位目标对象并抑制无关信息。然而，这种基于图像块的处理方式可能会将完整对象分割到多个图像块中，从而破坏语义相似度的计算。在我们的实验中，我们发现不同大小的对象图像块在不同分辨率下处理效果更好。基于这一观察，我们提出了多分辨率检索-检测（MRD），这是一个用于高分辨率图像理解的无需训练框架。为了解决对象被分割到不同图像块导致的语义相似性偏差问题，我们提出了一种多分辨率语义融合方法，该方法整合在不同分辨率下获得的语义相似度图，以产生更准确的语义信息并保持目标对象的完整性。此外，为了实现全局尺度的直接目标对象定位，我们引入了一个开放词汇目标检测（OVD）模型，该模型使用滑动窗口方法识别对象区域。在不同MLLMs上进行的高分辨率图像理解基准测试实验证明了我们方法的有效性。

### [74] [DiverseAR: Boosting Diversity in Bitwise Autoregressive Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02931)
*Ying Yang,Zhengyao Lv,Tianlin Pan,Haofan Wang,Binxin Yang,Hubery Yin,Chen Li,Chenyang Si*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DiverseAR通过自适应逻辑分布缩放和能量路径搜索，解决了比特自回归图像生成中多样性不足的问题，在保持视觉质量的同时显著提升样本多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究比特自回归生成模型中样本多样性不足的问题，识别出二元分类特性和尖锐逻辑分布是限制多样性的关键因素。

Method: 提出自适应逻辑分布缩放机制动态调整输出分布尖锐度，并结合能量基生成路径搜索算法避免低置信度标记采样。

Result: 实验证明DiverseAR显著提升了比特自回归图像生成的样本多样性，同时保持了高视觉质量。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the underexplored challenge of sample diversity in autoregressive (AR) generative models with bitwise visual tokenizers. We first analyze the factors that limit diversity in bitwise AR models and identify two key issues: (1) the binary classification nature of bitwise modeling, which restricts the prediction space, and (2) the overly sharp logits distribution, which causes sampling collapse and reduces diversity. Building on these insights, we propose DiverseAR, a principled and effective method that enhances image diversity without sacrificing visual quality. Specifically, we introduce an adaptive logits distribution scaling mechanism that dynamically adjusts the sharpness of the binary output distribution during sampling, resulting in smoother predictions and greater diversity. To mitigate potential fidelity loss caused by distribution smoothing, we further develop an energy-based generation path search algorithm that avoids sampling low-confidence tokens, thereby preserving high visual quality. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DiverseAR substantially improves sample diversity in bitwise autoregressive image generation.

中文标题: DiverseAR：提升比特自回归图像生成多样性的方法

### [75] [EGGS: Exchangeable 2D/3D Gaussian Splatting for Geometry-Appearance Balanced Novel View Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02932)
*Yancheng Zhang,Guangyu Sun,Chen Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EGGS提出了一种混合2D/3D高斯泼溅表示，通过自适应类型交换和频率解耦优化，平衡了渲染质量与几何精度，解决了现有方法在一致性和细节间的权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有新视角合成方法存在权衡问题：3DGS虽然渲染质量高但几何一致性差，2DGS几何一致性好但纹理细节不足。需要一种能同时保持高质量外观和准确几何的方法。

Method: 1. 混合高斯光栅化：统一渲染2D和3D高斯表示；2. 自适应类型交换：根据场景需求动态转换高斯类型；3. 频率解耦优化：分别优化低频几何和高频纹理；4. CUDA加速实现。

Result: 实验表明EGGS在渲染质量、几何精度和效率方面优于现有方法，实现了外观与几何的良好平衡，同时保持实时渲染能力。

Conclusion: EGGS通过创新的混合高斯表示和优化策略，成功解决了新视角合成中外观质量与几何精度之间的权衡问题，为高质量实时渲染提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Novel view synthesis (NVS) is crucial in computer vision and graphics, with wide applications in AR, VR, and autonomous driving. While 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) enables real-time rendering with high appearance fidelity, it suffers from multi-view inconsistencies, limiting geometric accuracy. In contrast, 2D Gaussian Splatting (2DGS) enforces multi-view consistency but compromises texture details. To address these limitations, we propose Exchangeable Gaussian Splatting (EGGS), a hybrid representation that integrates 2D and 3D Gaussians to balance appearance and geometry. To achieve this, we introduce Hybrid Gaussian Rasterization for unified rendering, Adaptive Type Exchange for dynamic adaptation between 2D and 3D Gaussians, and Frequency-Decoupled Optimization that effectively exploits the strengths of each type of Gaussian representation. Our CUDA-accelerated implementation ensures efficient training and inference. Extensive experiments demonstrate that EGGS outperforms existing methods in rendering quality, geometric accuracy, and efficiency, providing a practical solution for high-quality NVS.

中文标题: EGGS：用于几何-外观平衡新视角合成的可交换2D/3D高斯泼溅

中文摘要: 新视角合成（NVS）在计算机视觉和图形学中至关重要，在增强现实、虚拟现实和自动驾驶等领域有广泛应用。虽然3D高斯泼溅（3DGS）能够实现实时渲染并具有高外观保真度，但它存在多视角不一致的问题，限制了几何精度。相比之下，2D高斯泼溅（2DGS）强制多视角一致性，但牺牲了纹理细节。为了解决这些限制，我们提出了可交换高斯泼溅（EGGS），这是一种混合表示方法，集成了2D和3D高斯函数来平衡外观和几何。为实现这一目标，我们引入了混合高斯光栅化以实现统一渲染，自适应类型交换以实现2D和3D高斯之间的动态适应，以及频率解耦优化，有效利用每种高斯表示的优势。我们的CUDA加速实现确保了高效的训练和推理。大量实验表明，EGGS在渲染质量、几何精度和效率方面优于现有方法，为高质量NVS提供了实用解决方案。

Motivation: 现有视频基准测试主要基于物理常识，无法充分评估视频模型对科学定律的理解和推理能力。视频生成的下一个前沿需要模型具备零样本科学推理能力，以准确建模现实世界的物理化学现象。

Method: 创建包含200个精心策划提示的基准测试，涵盖14个物理化学主题和103个概念。每个提示编码复合科学场景，需要理解多个科学概念。使用专家注释评估七个最先进视频模型，从五个维度（提示一致性、现象一致性、正确动态性、不变性、时空连续性）进行评估，并采用VLM-as-a-Judge方法进行自动化评估。

Result: VLM-as-a-Judge评估方法与人类专家评估结果呈现强相关性，验证了自动化评估方法的有效性。基准测试成功评估了视频模型作为科学推理器的能力，而不仅仅是生成器。

Conclusion: VideoScience-Bench是首个专门评估视频模型科学理解和推理能力的基准测试，填补了现有评估体系的空白，为视频生成模型的科学推理能力提供了系统化的评估框架。

Abstract: The next frontier for video generation lies in developing models capable of zero-shot reasoning, where understanding real-world scientific laws is crucial for accurate physical outcome modeling under diverse conditions. However, existing video benchmarks are physical commonsense-based, offering limited insight into video models' scientific reasoning capability. We introduce VideoScience-Bench, a benchmark designed to evaluate undergraduate-level scientific understanding in video models. Each prompt encodes a composite scientific scenario that requires understanding and reasoning across multiple scientific concepts to generate the correct phenomenon. The benchmark comprises 200 carefully curated prompts spanning 14 topics and 103 concepts in physics and chemistry. We conduct expert-annotated evaluations across seven state-of-the-art video models in T2V and I2V settings along five dimensions: Prompt Consistency, Phenomenon Congruency, Correct Dynamism, Immutability, and Spatio-Temporal Continuity. Using a VLM-as-a-Judge to assess video generations, we observe strong correlation with human assessments. To the best of our knowledge, VideoScience-Bench is the first benchmark to evaluate video models not only as generators but also as reasoners, requiring their generations to demonstrate scientific understanding consistent with expected physical and chemical phenomena. Our data and evaluation code are available at: \href{https://github.com/hao-ai-lab/VideoScience}{github.com/hao-ai-lab/VideoScience}.

中文标题: 使用VideoScience-Bench对视频生成的科学理解与推理能力进行基准测试

中文摘要: 视频生成的下一个前沿在于开发能够进行零样本推理的模型，其中理解现实世界的科学定律对于在不同条件下准确建模物理结果至关重要。然而，现有的视频基准测试主要基于物理常识，对视频模型的科学推理能力提供有限洞察。我们引入了VideoScience-Bench，这是一个旨在评估视频模型中本科水平科学理解能力的基准测试。每个提示都编码了一个复合科学场景，需要理解和推理多个科学概念才能生成正确的现象。该基准测试包含200个精心策划的提示，涵盖物理和化学领域的14个主题和103个概念。我们在T2V和I2V设置下对七个最先进的视频模型进行了专家注释评估，涵盖五个维度：提示一致性、现象一致性、正确动态性、不变性和时空连续性。使用VLM-as-a-Judge评估视频生成，我们观察到与人类评估的强相关性。据我们所知，VideoScience-Bench是第一个不仅将视频模型评估为生成器，还评估为推理器的基准测试，要求其生成结果展示与预期物理和化学现象一致的科学理解。我们的数据和评估代码可在github.com/hao-ai-lab/VideoScience获取。

### [78] [Layout Anything: One Transformer for Universal Room Layout Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02952)
*Md Sohag Mia,Muhammad Abdullah Adnan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Layout Anything是一个基于Transformer的室内布局估计框架，采用OneFormer的通用分割架构进行几何结构预测，通过布局退化策略和可微分几何损失实现高效布局估计，在多个基准测试中达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 室内布局估计对于增强现实和大规模3D场景重建至关重要，但现有方法通常需要复杂的后处理流程且计算效率不高。本文旨在开发一个端到端的通用框架，既能保持几何一致性，又能实现高效推理。

Method: 采用OneFormer的通用分割架构，结合任务条件查询和对比学习。创新性地引入两个关键模块：1）布局退化策略，通过拓扑感知变换增强训练数据同时保持曼哈顿世界约束；2）可微分几何损失，在训练中直接强制平面一致性和锐利边界预测。

Result: 在多个标准基准测试中达到最先进性能：LSUN数据集上像素误差5.43%，角点误差4.02%；Hedau数据集上像素误差7.04%，角点误差5.17%；Matterport3D-Layout数据集上像素误差4.03%，角点误差3.15%。推理速度达到114ms，无需复杂后处理。

Conclusion: Layout Anything成功地将几何感知与计算效率相结合，为增强现实应用和大规模3D场景重建任务提供了高效实用的解决方案，消除了复杂的后处理流程，实现了端到端的室内布局估计。

Abstract: We present Layout Anything, a transformer-based framework for indoor layout estimation that adapts the OneFormer's universal segmentation architecture to geometric structure prediction. Our approach integrates OneFormer's task-conditioned queries and contrastive learning with two key modules: (1) a layout degeneration strategy that augments training data while preserving Manhattan-world constraints through topology-aware transformations, and (2) differentiable geometric losses that directly enforce planar consistency and sharp boundary predictions during training. By unifying these components in an end-to-end framework, the model eliminates complex post-processing pipelines while achieving high-speed inference at 114ms. Extensive experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across standard benchmarks, with pixel error (PE) of 5.43% and corner error (CE) of 4.02% on the LSUN, PE of 7.04% (CE 5.17%) on the Hedau and PE of 4.03% (CE 3.15%) on the Matterport3D-Layout datasets. The framework's combination of geometric awareness and computational efficiency makes it particularly suitable for augmented reality applications and large-scale 3D scene reconstruction tasks.

中文标题: 布局万物：用于通用房间布局估计的统一Transformer

### [79] [Contextual Image Attack: How Visual Context Exposes Multimodal Safety Vulnerabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02973)
*Yuan Xiong,Ziqi Miao,Lijun Li,Chen Qian,Jie Li,Jing Shao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的图像中心攻击方法CIA，通过多智能体系统将有害查询嵌入看似良性的视觉上下文中，利用四种可视化策略，显著提高了对多模态大语言模型的安全攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大语言模型安全攻击方法主要关注文本-图像交互，将视觉模态作为次要提示，未能充分利用图像承载复杂上下文信息的独特潜力。本文旨在填补这一空白，探索视觉模态本身作为攻击向量的有效性。

Method: 提出上下文图像攻击(CIA)方法，采用多智能体系统，通过四种不同的可视化策略将有害查询微妙地嵌入看似良性的视觉上下文中。系统还结合了上下文元素增强和自动毒性混淆技术来进一步提高攻击效果。

Result: 在MMSafetyBench-tiny数据集上的实验结果显示，CIA对GPT-4o和Qwen2.5-VL-72B模型分别获得了4.73和4.83的高毒性分数，攻击成功率分别达到86.31%和91.07%。该方法显著优于先前的工作。

Conclusion: 视觉模态本身是攻击先进多模态大语言模型的有效向量，CIA方法通过充分利用图像的上下文信息，成功暴露了多模态模型的安全漏洞。

Abstract: While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) show remarkable capabilities, their safety alignments are susceptible to jailbreak attacks. Existing attack methods typically focus on text-image interplay, treating the visual modality as a secondary prompt. This approach underutilizes the unique potential of images to carry complex, contextual information. To address this gap, we propose a new image-centric attack method, Contextual Image Attack (CIA), which employs a multi-agent system to subtly embeds harmful queries into seemingly benign visual contexts using four distinct visualization strategies. To further enhance the attack's efficacy, the system incorporate contextual element enhancement and automatic toxicity obfuscation techniques. Experimental results on the MMSafetyBench-tiny dataset show that CIA achieves high toxicity scores of 4.73 and 4.83 against the GPT-4o and Qwen2.5-VL-72B models, respectively, with Attack Success Rates (ASR) reaching 86.31\% and 91.07\%. Our method significantly outperforms prior work, demonstrating that the visual modality itself is a potent vector for jailbreaking advanced MLLMs.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常依赖人工干预或未能充分利用智能体自主缓解幻觉的能力。受人类在现实世界中做出可靠决策的认知过程启发——先通过内省推理减少不确定性形成初步判断，然后依赖外部多视角验证做出最终决定。

Method: 提出训练免费的多智能体框架InEx，包含内部内省推理（基于熵的不确定性估计指导）和外部跨模态多智能体协作。决策智能体首先生成响应，然后通过编辑智能体和自反思智能体的迭代验证与精炼来增强可靠性。

Result: 在通用和幻觉基准测试上持续优于现有方法，获得4%-27%的性能增益，并展现出强大的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: InEx通过模仿人类认知决策过程，有效缓解了多模态大语言模型的幻觉问题，为构建更可靠的AI系统提供了新思路。

Abstract: Hallucination remains a critical challenge in large language models (LLMs), hindering the development of reliable multimodal LLMs (MLLMs). Existing solutions often rely on human intervention or underutilize the agent's ability to autonomously mitigate hallucination. To address these limitations, we draw inspiration from how humans make reliable decisions in the real world. They begin with introspective reasoning to reduce uncertainty and form an initial judgment, then rely on external verification from diverse perspectives to reach a final decision. Motivated by this cognitive paradigm, we propose InEx, a training-free, multi-agent framework designed to autonomously mitigate hallucination. InEx introduces internal introspective reasoning, guided by entropy-based uncertainty estimation, to improve the reliability of the decision agent's reasoning process. The agent first generates a response, which is then iteratively verified and refined through external cross-modal multi-agent collaboration with the editing agent and self-reflection agents, further enhancing reliability and mitigating hallucination. Extensive experiments show that InEx consistently outperforms existing methods, achieving 4%-27% gains on general and hallucination benchmarks, and demonstrating strong robustness.

中文标题: InEx：通过内省和跨模态多智能体协作缓解幻觉

中文摘要: 幻觉仍然是大型语言模型（LLMs）面临的关键挑战，阻碍了可靠多模态LLMs（MLLMs）的发展。现有解决方案通常依赖人工干预或未能充分利用智能体自主缓解幻觉的能力。为了解决这些限制，我们受到人类在现实世界中做出可靠决策方式的启发。他们首先通过内省推理减少不确定性并形成初步判断，然后依赖来自不同视角的外部验证来做出最终决定。受这种认知范式的启发，我们提出了InEx，一个无需训练的多智能体框架，旨在自主缓解幻觉。InEx引入了内部内省推理，基于熵的不确定性估计指导，以提高决策智能体推理过程的可靠性。智能体首先生成响应，然后通过编辑智能体和自反思智能体的外部跨模态多智能体协作进行迭代验证和精炼，进一步增强可靠性并缓解幻觉。大量实验表明，InEx在通用和幻觉基准测试上持续优于现有方法，实现了4%-27%的性能提升，并展现出强大的鲁棒性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出自适应跨模态Transformer(ACMT)将图像特征自适应地集成到点表示中；引入图推理模块(GRM)通过多尺度图注意力建模邻域关系；采用级联解码器进行多阶段预测细化。

Our approach introduces the Adaptive Cross-Modal Transformer (ACMT), which adaptively integrates image features into point representations to enrich both geometric and semantic information. *Kairun Wen,Yuzhi Huang,Runyu Chen,Hui Zheng,Yunlong Lin,Panwang Pan,Chenxin Li,Wenyan Cong,Jian Zhang,Junbin Lu,Chenguo Lin,Dilin Wang,Zhicheng Yan,Hongyu Xu,Justin Theiss,Yue Huang,Xinghao Ding,Rakesh Ranjan,Zhiwen Fan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DynamicVerse是一个物理感知的多模态4D世界建模框架，通过整合大型视觉、几何和多模态模型，将真实世界视频转换为包含度量尺度几何、动态运动、实例掩码和描述性标注的全面4D表示，创建了大规模数据集并在多个基准任务上表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数据集存在局限性：大多来自有限模拟器或使用传统运动结构恢复方法，标注尺度有限且描述性标注不足，导致基础模型难以从互联网单目视频中准确理解真实世界的动态物理特性，限制了具身智能体在真实环境中的感知和交互能力。

Method: 采用大型视觉、几何和多模态模型解析视频内容；结合基于窗口的束调整与全局优化技术；将长视频序列转换为包含度量尺度静态几何、真实世界动态运动、实例级掩码和整体描述性标注的4D多模态格式。

Result: 构建了包含10万+视频、80万+标注掩码和1000万+帧的大规模数据集；在视频深度估计、相机姿态估计和相机内参估计三个基准任务上表现出优于现有方法的性能，特别是在捕捉物理尺度测量方面具有更高的全局精度。

Conclusion: DynamicVerse成功填补了现有数据集的不足，提供了一个物理感知的多模态4D世界建模框架，能够从真实世界视频中准确提取动态物理特性，为具身智能体在真实环境中的感知和交互提供了重要基础，在多个基准任务上验证了其有效性。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamic physical world, characterized by its evolving 3D structure, real-world motion, and semantic content with textual descriptions, is crucial for human-agent interaction and enables embodied agents to perceive and act within real environments with human-like capabilities. However, existing datasets are often derived from limited simulators or utilize traditional Structurefrom-Motion for up-to-scale annotation and offer limited descriptive captioning, which restricts the capacity of foundation models to accurately interpret real-world dynamics from monocular videos, commonly sourced from the internet. To bridge these gaps, we introduce DynamicVerse, a physical-scale, multimodal 4D world modeling framework for dynamic real-world video. We employ large vision, geometric, and multimodal models to interpret metric-scale static geometry, real-world dynamic motion, instance-level masks, and holistic descriptive captions. By integrating window-based Bundle Adjustment with global optimization, our method converts long real-world video sequences into a comprehensive 4D multimodal format. DynamicVerse delivers a large-scale dataset consists of 100K+ videos with 800K+ annotated masks and 10M+ frames from internet videos. Experimental evaluations on three benchmark tasks, namely video depth estimation, camera pose estimation, and camera intrinsics estimation, demonstrate that our 4D modeling achieves superior performance in capturing physical-scale measurements with greater global accuracy than existing methods.

中文标题: DynamicVerse：一种物理感知的多模态4D世界建模框架

中文摘要: 理解动态物理世界，其特征包括不断演化的3D结构、真实世界运动以及带有文本描述的语义内容，对于人机交互至关重要，并使具身智能体能够以类人能力感知和作用于真实环境。然而，现有数据集通常源自有限的模拟器或使用传统的运动结构恢复进行尺度标注，且提供有限的描述性标注，这限制了基础模型从通常来自互联网的单目视频中准确解释真实世界动态的能力。为弥合这些差距，我们引入了DynamicVerse，一个用于动态真实世界视频的物理尺度多模态4D世界建模框架。我们采用大型视觉、几何和多模态模型来解释度量尺度的静态几何、真实世界动态运动、实例级掩码和整体描述性标注。通过将基于窗口的束调整与全局优化相结合，我们的方法将长真实世界视频序列转换为全面的4D多模态格式。DynamicVerse提供了一个大规模数据集，包含来自互联网视频的10万+视频、80万+标注掩码和1000万+帧。在三个基准任务（视频深度估计、相机姿态估计和相机内参估计）上的实验评估表明，我们的4D建模在捕捉物理尺度测量方面实现了优于现有方法的性能，具有更高的全局精度。

### [84] [DGGT: Feedforward 4D Reconstruction of Dynamic Driving Scenes using Unposed Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03004)
*Xiaoxue Chen,Ziyi Xiong,Yuantao Chen,Gen Li,Nan Wang,Hongcheng Luo,Long Chen,Haiyang Sun,Bing Wang,Guang Chen,Hangjun Ye,Hongyang Li,Ya-Qin Zhang,Hao Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DGGT是一个前馈式框架，能够直接从稀疏、未标定图像重建动态驾驶场景，无需相机姿态输入，支持任意视图数量和长序列，实现了最先进的4D重建性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶需要快速、可扩展的4D重建和重模拟用于训练和评估，但现有方法依赖每场景优化、已知相机标定或短帧窗口，导致速度慢且不实用。现有方法将相机姿态作为必需输入限制了灵活性和可扩展性。

Method: 提出Driving Gaussian Grounded Transformer (DGGT)统一框架：1）将相机姿态重新定义为模型输出而非输入；2）联合预测每帧3D高斯图和相机参数；3）使用轻量级动态头解耦动态；4）通过寿命头调节时间可见性保持时间一致性；5）基于扩散的渲染细化减少运动伪影。

Result: 在Waymo、nuScenes、Argoverse2等大型驾驶基准上，DGGT在单数据集训练和跨数据集零样本迁移中都优于先前工作，随着输入帧数增加具有良好的扩展性，实现了最先进的性能和速度。

Conclusion: DGGT通过将相机姿态重新定义为输出而非输入，实现了直接从稀疏未标定图像进行动态驾驶场景重建，解决了现有方法的灵活性和可扩展性限制，为自动驾驶的4D重建和重模拟提供了高效实用的解决方案。

Abstract: Autonomous driving needs fast, scalable 4D reconstruction and re-simulation for training and evaluation, yet most methods for dynamic driving scenes still rely on per-scene optimization, known camera calibration, or short frame windows, making them slow and impractical. We revisit this problem from a feedforward perspective and introduce \textbf{Driving Gaussian Grounded Transformer (DGGT)}, a unified framework for pose-free dynamic scene reconstruction. We note that the existing formulations, treating camera pose as a required input, limit flexibility and scalability. Instead, we reformulate pose as an output of the model, enabling reconstruction directly from sparse, unposed images and supporting an arbitrary number of views for long sequences. Our approach jointly predicts per-frame 3D Gaussian maps and camera parameters, disentangles dynamics with a lightweight dynamic head, and preserves temporal consistency with a lifespan head that modulates visibility over time. A diffusion-based rendering refinement further reduces motion/interpolation artifacts and improves novel-view quality under sparse inputs. The result is a single-pass, pose-free algorithm that achieves state-of-the-art performance and speed. Trained and evaluated on large-scale driving benchmarks (Waymo, nuScenes, Argoverse2), our method outperforms prior work both when trained on each dataset and in zero-shot transfer across datasets, and it scales well as the number of input frames increases.

中文标题: DGGT：使用未标定图像的动态驾驶场景前馈式4D重建

中文摘要: 自动驾驶需要快速、可扩展的4D重建和重模拟用于训练和评估，然而大多数动态驾驶场景方法仍然依赖于每场景优化、已知相机标定或短帧窗口，使得它们速度慢且不实用。我们从前馈角度重新审视这个问题，并引入了**驾驶高斯接地变换器（DGGT）**，这是一个用于无姿态动态场景重建的统一框架。我们注意到现有方法将相机姿态视为必需输入，限制了灵活性和可扩展性。相反，我们将姿态重新定义为模型的输出，从而能够直接从稀疏、未标定的图像进行重建，并支持任意数量的视图用于长序列。我们的方法联合预测每帧3D高斯图和相机参数，通过轻量级动态头解耦动态，并通过寿命头在时间上调节可见性来保持时间一致性。基于扩散的渲染细化进一步减少了运动/插值伪影，并改善了稀疏输入下的新视角质量。结果是一个单次通过、无姿态的算法，实现了最先进的性能和速度。在大型驾驶基准（Waymo、nuScenes、Argoverse2）上进行训练和评估，我们的方法在分别在每个数据集上训练时以及在跨数据集的零样本迁移中都优于先前工作，并且随着输入帧数的增加而具有良好的扩展性。

### [85] [In-Context Sync-LoRA for Portrait Video Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03013)
*Sagi Polaczek,Or Patashnik,Ali Mahdavi-Amiri,Daniel Cohen-Or*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Sync-LoRA是一种基于图像到视频扩散模型的肖像视频编辑方法，通过训练上下文LoRA实现帧级精确同步，在保持原始运动轨迹的同时实现高质量视觉编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 肖像视频编辑需要在保持原始时间行为的同时实现灵活控制，现有方法难以平衡编辑保真度和运动同步，导致编辑帧与源帧不同步或身份不一致的问题。

Method: 使用图像到视频扩散模型，通过修改第一帧定义编辑并传播到整个序列；训练上下文LoRA使用自动生成的同步视频对，这些视频对具有相同运动轨迹但不同外观；采用同步过滤机制筛选高质量训练数据。

Result: Sync-LoRA能够处理多样化的编辑任务（外观修改、添加对象、背景更改），在未见过的身份上表现出良好的泛化能力，保持高视觉保真度和强时间一致性，实现编辑保真度与运动保持的平衡。

Conclusion: Sync-LoRA通过上下文LoRA训练和同步数据筛选，有效解决了肖像视频编辑中的时间同步挑战，为高质量、帧级精确的视频编辑提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Editing portrait videos is a challenging task that requires flexible yet precise control over a wide range of modifications, such as appearance changes, expression edits, or the addition of objects. The key difficulty lies in preserving the subject's original temporal behavior, demanding that every edited frame remains precisely synchronized with the corresponding source frame. We present Sync-LoRA, a method for editing portrait videos that achieves high-quality visual modifications while maintaining frame-accurate synchronization and identity consistency. Our approach uses an image-to-video diffusion model, where the edit is defined by modifying the first frame and then propagated to the entire sequence. To enable accurate synchronization, we train an in-context LoRA using paired videos that depict identical motion trajectories but differ in appearance. These pairs are automatically generated and curated through a synchronization-based filtering process that selects only the most temporally aligned examples for training. This training setup teaches the model to combine motion cues from the source video with the visual changes introduced in the edited first frame. Trained on a compact, highly curated set of synchronized human portraits, Sync-LoRA generalizes to unseen identities and diverse edits (e.g., modifying appearance, adding objects, or changing backgrounds), robustly handling variations in pose and expression. Our results demonstrate high visual fidelity and strong temporal coherence, achieving a robust balance between edit fidelity and precise motion preservation.

中文标题: 上下文同步LoRA用于肖像视频编辑

中文摘要: 编辑肖像视频是一项具有挑战性的任务，需要在保持原始时间行为的同时实现灵活而精确的控制，如外观变化、表情编辑或添加对象。主要困难在于保持主体的原始时间行为，要求每个编辑帧与对应的源帧保持精确同步。我们提出了Sync-LoRA，一种用于编辑肖像视频的方法，在保持帧级精确同步和身份一致性的同时实现高质量的视觉修改。我们的方法使用图像到视频扩散模型，其中编辑通过修改第一帧然后传播到整个序列来定义。为了实现精确同步，我们使用描绘相同运动轨迹但外观不同的配对视频训练一个上下文LoRA。这些配对通过基于同步的过滤过程自动生成和筛选，仅选择最时间对齐的示例进行训练。这种训练设置教会模型将源视频的运动线索与编辑第一帧引入的视觉变化相结合。在紧凑、高度筛选的同步人类肖像数据集上训练后，Sync-LoRA能够泛化到未见过的身份和多样化的编辑（如修改外观、添加对象或更改背景），稳健地处理姿势和表情的变化。我们的结果展示了高视觉保真度和强时间一致性，在编辑保真度和精确运动保持之间实现了稳健的平衡。

### [86] [AutoBrep: Autoregressive B-Rep Generation with Unified Topology and Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03018)
*Xiang Xu,Pradeep Kumar Jayaraman,Joseph G. Lambourne,Yilin Liu,Durvesh Malpure,Pete Meltzer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AutoBrep是一种基于Transformer的自回归模型，通过统一的标记化方案同时编码B-Rep的几何和拓扑信息，能够生成高质量、水密的CAD边界表示模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界表示（B-Rep）是CAD中的标准数据结构，但现有方法难以直接生成具有精确几何和水密拓扑的B-Rep。需要一种能够同时处理几何和拓扑的统一生成方法。

Method: 1. 使用统一的标记化方案将B-Rep的几何基元（曲面和曲线）编码为潜在几何标记，拓扑关系编码为特殊引用标记。2. 采用Transformer架构进行自回归生成。3. 序列顺序遵循B-Rep面邻接图的广度优先遍历。4. 在推理时逐步生成相邻的面、边及其拓扑结构。

Result: 1. 在质量和拓扑水密性方面优于基线方法。2. 具有良好的可扩展性，能够处理复杂实体。3. 推理速度快。4. 原生支持B-Rep自动完成功能，实现用户可控的CAD生成。

Conclusion: AutoBrep通过统一的几何-拓扑表示和自回归生成框架，成功解决了B-Rep生成中的质量和拓扑完整性挑战，为CAD模型生成提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: The boundary representation (B-Rep) is the standard data structure used in Computer-Aided Design (CAD) for defining solid models. Despite recent progress, directly generating B-Reps end-to-end with precise geometry and watertight topology remains a challenge. This paper presents AutoBrep, a novel Transformer model that autoregressively generates B-Reps with high quality and validity. AutoBrep employs a unified tokenization scheme that encodes both geometric and topological characteristics of a B-Rep model as a sequence of discrete tokens. Geometric primitives (i.e., surfaces and curves) are encoded as latent geometry tokens, and their structural relationships are defined as special topological reference tokens. Sequence order in AutoBrep naturally follows a breadth first traversal of the B-Rep face adjacency graph. At inference time, neighboring faces and edges along with their topological structure are progressively generated. Extensive experiments demonstrate the advantages of our unified representation when coupled with next-token prediction for B-Rep generation. AutoBrep outperforms baselines with better quality and watertightness. It is also highly scalable to complex solids with good fidelity and inference speed. We further show that autocompleting B-Reps is natively supported through our unified tokenization, enabling user-controllable CAD generation with minimal changes. Code is available at https://github.com/AutodeskAILab/AutoBrep.

中文标题: AutoBrep：具有统一拓扑与几何的自回归B-Rep生成方法

中文摘要: 边界表示（B-Rep）是计算机辅助设计（CAD）中定义实体模型的标准数据结构。尽管最近取得了一些进展，但直接端到端生成具有精确几何和水密拓扑的B-Rep仍然是一个挑战。本文提出了AutoBrep，一种新颖的Transformer模型，能够自回归地生成高质量且有效的B-Rep。AutoBrep采用统一的标记化方案，将B-Rep模型的几何和拓扑特征编码为离散标记序列。几何基元（即曲面和曲线）被编码为潜在几何标记，它们的结构关系被定义为特殊的拓扑引用标记。AutoBrep中的序列顺序自然遵循B-Rep面邻接图的广度优先遍历。在推理时，相邻的面和边及其拓扑结构被逐步生成。大量实验证明了我们的统一表示与下一标记预测相结合在B-Rep生成中的优势。AutoBrep在质量和水密性方面优于基线方法。它还具有高度可扩展性，能够处理复杂实体，具有良好的保真度和推理速度。我们进一步展示了通过我们的统一标记化原生支持B-Rep的自动完成功能，实现了用户可控的CAD生成，只需最小改动。代码可在https://github.com/AutodeskAILab/AutoBrep获取。

### [87] [MAViD: A Multimodal Framework for Audio-Visual Dialogue Understanding and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03034)
*Youxin Pang,Jiajun Liu,Lingfeng Tan,Yong Zhang,Feng Gao,Xiang Deng,Zhuoliang Kang,Xiaoming Wei,Yebin Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MAViD是一个用于音视频对话理解和生成的多模态框架，采用Conductor-Creator架构，通过分离理解和生成任务，结合自回归和扩散模型，实现高质量、长时长的音视频对话生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法主要关注非交互式系统，生成受限且不自然的人类语音。主要挑战在于有效整合理解和生成能力，以及实现无缝的多模态音视频融合。

Method: 提出Conductor-Creator架构：Conductor负责理解、推理和生成指令，将指令分解为动作和语音组件；Creator基于指令生成交互响应。采用自回归模型生成音频，扩散模型生成高质量视频，并提出新颖的融合模块增强连续片段和多模态间的连接。

Result: 大量实验表明，该框架能够生成生动且上下文连贯的长时长对话交互，并能准确解释用户的多模态查询。

Conclusion: MAViD框架通过创新的架构设计，成功解决了音视频对话理解和生成中的关键挑战，实现了高质量、长时长的多模态对话交互。

Abstract: We propose MAViD, a novel Multimodal framework for Audio-Visual Dialogue understanding and generation. Existing approaches primarily focus on non-interactive systems and are limited to producing constrained and unnatural human speech.The primary challenge of this task lies in effectively integrating understanding and generation capabilities, as well as achieving seamless multimodal audio-video fusion. To solve these problems, we propose a Conductor-Creator architecture that divides the dialogue system into two primary components.The Conductor is tasked with understanding, reasoning, and generating instructions by breaking them down into motion and speech components, thereby enabling fine-grained control over interactions. The Creator then delivers interactive responses based on these instructions.Furthermore, to address the difficulty of generating long videos with consistent identity, timbre, and tone using dual DiT structures, the Creator adopts a structure that combines autoregressive (AR) and diffusion models. The AR model is responsible for audio generation, while the diffusion model ensures high-quality video generation.Additionally, we propose a novel fusion module to enhance connections between contextually consecutive clips and modalities, enabling synchronized long-duration audio-visual content generation.Extensive experiments demonstrate that our framework can generate vivid and contextually coherent long-duration dialogue interactions and accurately interpret users' multimodal queries.

中文标题: MAViD：用于音视频对话理解和生成的多模态框架

中文摘要: 我们提出了MAViD，一个用于音视频对话理解和生成的新型多模态框架。现有方法主要关注非交互式系统，且局限于生成受限和不自然的人类语音。该任务的主要挑战在于有效整合理解和生成能力，以及实现无缝的多模态音视频融合。为解决这些问题，我们提出了Conductor-Creator架构，将对话系统分为两个主要组件。Conductor负责理解、推理和生成指令，通过将指令分解为动作和语音组件，实现对交互的细粒度控制。Creator然后基于这些指令生成交互响应。此外，为解决使用双重DiT结构生成具有一致身份、音色和语调的长视频的困难，Creator采用了结合自回归（AR）和扩散模型的结构。AR模型负责音频生成，而扩散模型确保高质量视频生成。另外，我们提出了新颖的融合模块来增强上下文连续片段和多模态间的连接，实现同步的长时长音视频内容生成。大量实验表明，我们的框架能够生成生动且上下文连贯的长时长对话交互，并能准确解释用户的多模态查询。

### [88] [ViSAudio: End-to-End Video-Driven Binaural Spatial Audio Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03036)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视频到音频生成领域主要关注单声道输出，缺乏空间沉浸感。现有的双耳音频方法采用两阶段管道（先生成单声道音频再进行空间化），导致误差累积和时空不一致问题。需要端到端的解决方案直接从视频生成双耳空间音频。

Method: 提出ViSAudio端到端框架：1）构建BiAudio数据集，包含约97K视频-双耳音频对，涵盖多样化真实场景和相机旋转轨迹；2）采用条件流匹配技术，设计双分支音频生成架构，两个专用分支分别建模音频潜在流；3）集成条件时空模块，平衡声道间一致性同时保留独特的空间特征，确保音频与输入视频的精确时空对齐。

Result: 综合实验表明，ViSAudio在客观指标和主观评估上都优于现有最先进方法，能够生成高质量的双耳音频，具有空间沉浸感，并能有效适应视角变化、声源运动和多样化声学环境。

Conclusion: ViSAudio成功实现了端到端的视频驱动双耳空间音频生成，通过创新的双分支架构和条件流匹配技术解决了现有方法的局限性，为沉浸式音频生成提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Despite progress in video-to-audio generation, the field focuses predominantly on mono output, lacking spatial immersion. Existing binaural approaches remain constrained by a two-stage pipeline that first generates mono audio and then performs spatialization, often resulting in error accumulation and spatio-temporal inconsistencies. To address this limitation, we introduce the task of end-to-end binaural spatial audio generation directly from silent video. To support this task, we present the BiAudio dataset, comprising approximately 97K video-binaural audio pairs spanning diverse real-world scenes and camera rotation trajectories, constructed through a semi-automated pipeline. Furthermore, we propose ViSAudio, an end-to-end framework that employs conditional flow matching with a dual-branch audio generation architecture, where two dedicated branches model the audio latent flows. Integrated with a conditional spacetime module, it balances consistency between channels while preserving distinctive spatial characteristics, ensuring precise spatio-temporal alignment between audio and the input video. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that ViSAudio outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods across both objective metrics and subjective evaluations, generating high-quality binaural audio with spatial immersion that adapts effectively to viewpoint changes, sound-source motion, and diverse acoustic environments. Project website: https://kszpxxzmc.github.io/ViSAudio-project.

中文标题: ViSAudio：端到端视频驱动的双耳空间音频生成

中文摘要: 尽管视频到音频生成领域取得了进展，但该领域主要关注单声道输出，缺乏空间沉浸感。现有的双耳方法仍然受限于两阶段管道，首先生成单声道音频，然后进行空间化，通常导致误差累积和时空不一致。为解决这一限制，我们引入了直接从无声视频端到端生成双耳空间音频的任务。为支持此任务，我们提出了BiAudio数据集，包含约97K视频-双耳音频对，涵盖多样化真实场景和相机旋转轨迹，通过半自动化管道构建。此外，我们提出了ViSAudio，一个端到端框架，采用条件流匹配和双分支音频生成架构，其中两个专用分支建模音频潜在流。与条件时空模块集成，它平衡声道间一致性，同时保留独特的空间特征，确保音频与输入视频的精确时空对齐。综合实验表明，ViSAudio在客观指标和主观评估上都优于现有最先进方法，生成高质量的双耳音频，具有空间沉浸感，并能有效适应视角变化、声源运动和多样化声学环境。项目网站：https://kszpxxzmc.github.io/ViSAudio-project。

Abstract: We investigate whether video generative models can exhibit visuospatial intelligence, a capability central to human cognition, using only visual data. Both tasks use video-only inputs, without auxiliary modalities such as depth or poses. ### [90] [MultiShotMaster: A Controllable Multi-Shot Video Generation Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03041)
*Qinghe Wang,Xiaoyu Shi,Baolu Li,Weikang Bian,Quande Liu,Huchuan Lu,Xintao Wang,Pengfei Wan,Kun Gai,Xu Jia*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MultiShotMaster是一个可控的多镜头视频生成框架，通过改进RoPE位置编码实现灵活的镜头安排、连贯叙事和时空控制，解决了现有方法难以生成叙事性多镜头视频的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视频生成技术擅长生成单镜头片段，但在生成叙事性多镜头视频方面存在困难。多镜头视频需要灵活的镜头安排、连贯的叙事以及超越文本提示的可控性。现有方法难以同时满足这些要求，且缺乏多镜头视频训练数据。

Method: 1. 扩展预训练的单镜头模型，集成两种新型RoPE变体：多镜头叙事RoPE（在镜头转换时应用显式相位偏移）和时空位置感知RoPE（结合参考标记和接地信号）。2. 建立自动化数据标注流程，从现有视频中提取多镜头视频、字幕、跨镜头接地信号和参考图像。3. 利用内在架构特性支持多镜头视频生成，包括文本驱动的镜头间一致性、自定义主体运动控制和背景驱动的自定义场景。

Result: 实验表明该框架在生成质量和可控性方面表现优异。能够灵活配置镜头数量和时长，实现文本驱动的镜头间一致性、自定义主体运动控制和背景驱动的自定义场景。相比现有方法，在多镜头视频生成任务上具有显著优势。

Conclusion: MultiShotMaster成功解决了多镜头视频生成的挑战，通过创新的RoPE变体和自动化数据标注流程，实现了高度可控的多镜头视频生成，为叙事性视频创作提供了强大的工具。

Abstract: Current video generation techniques excel at single-shot clips but struggle to produce narrative multi-shot videos, which require flexible shot arrangement, coherent narrative, and controllability beyond text prompts. To tackle these challenges, we propose MultiShotMaster, a framework for highly controllable multi-shot video generation. We extend a pretrained single-shot model by integrating two novel variants of RoPE. First, we introduce Multi-Shot Narrative RoPE, which applies explicit phase shift at shot transitions, enabling flexible shot arrangement while preserving the temporal narrative order. Second, we design Spatiotemporal Position-Aware RoPE to incorporate reference tokens and grounding signals, enabling spatiotemporal-grounded reference injection. In addition, to overcome data scarcity, we establish an automated data annotation pipeline to extract multi-shot videos, captions, cross-shot grounding signals and reference images. Our framework leverages the intrinsic architectural properties to support multi-shot video generation, featuring text-driven inter-shot consistency, customized subject with motion control, and background-driven customized scene. Both shot count and duration are flexibly configurable. Extensive experiments demonstrate the superior performance and outstanding controllability of our framework.

中文标题: MultiShotMaster：一个可控的多镜头视频生成框架

中文摘要: 当前的视频生成技术擅长生成单镜头片段，但在生成叙事性多镜头视频方面存在困难，这需要灵活的镜头安排、连贯的叙事以及超越文本提示的可控性。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出了MultiShotMaster，一个用于高度可控多镜头视频生成的框架。我们通过集成两种新型RoPE变体来扩展预训练的单镜头模型。首先，我们引入了多镜头叙事RoPE，它在镜头转换时应用显式相位偏移，实现了灵活的镜头安排同时保持了时间叙事顺序。其次，我们设计了时空位置感知RoPE，以结合参考标记和接地信号，实现时空接地的参考注入。此外，为了克服数据稀缺问题，我们建立了一个自动化数据标注流程，用于提取多镜头视频、字幕、跨镜头接地信号和参考图像。我们的框架利用内在架构特性来支持多镜头视频生成，具有文本驱动的镜头间一致性、自定义主体运动控制和背景驱动的自定义场景等特点。镜头数量和时长均可灵活配置。大量实验证明了我们框架的卓越性能和出色的可控性。

### [91] [OneThinker: All-in-one Reasoning Model for Image and Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03043)
*Kaituo Feng,Manyuan Zhang,Hongyu Li,Kaixuan Fan,Shuang Chen,Yilei Jiang,Dian Zheng,Peiwen Sun,Yiyuan Zhang,Haoze Sun,Yan Feng,Peng Pei,Xunliang Cai,Xiangyu Yue*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OneThinker是一个统一的多模态推理模型，能够同时处理图像和视频的多种视觉任务，包括问答、描述、定位、跟踪和分割，通过多任务强化学习和大规模训练数据实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常为不同视觉任务训练单独模型，将图像和视频推理视为独立领域，限制了向多模态推理通用模型的发展，阻碍了跨任务和跨模态的知识共享。

Method: 1. 构建OneThinker-600k训练语料库，涵盖多种视觉任务；2. 使用商业模型进行思维链标注，得到OneThinker-SFT-340k用于监督微调冷启动；3. 提出EMA-GRPO方法处理多任务强化学习中的奖励异质性，通过跟踪任务奖励标准差的移动平均值实现平衡优化。

Result: 在31个视觉基准测试中表现出色，涵盖10个基础视觉理解任务；展现出任务间的有效知识转移和初步的零样本泛化能力。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has recently achieved remarkable success in eliciting visual reasoning within Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs). However, existing approaches typically train separate models for different tasks and treat image and video reasoning as disjoint domains. This results in limited scalability toward a multimodal reasoning generalist, which restricts practical versatility and hinders potential knowledge sharing across tasks and modalities. To achieve this, we construct the OneThinker-600k training corpus covering all these tasks and employ commercial models for CoT annotation, resulting in OneThinker-SFT-340k for SFT cold start. ### [92] [CAMEO: Correspondence-Attention Alignment for Multi-View Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03045)
*Minkyung Kwon,Jinhyeok Choi,Jiho Park,Seonghu Jeon,Jinhyuk Jang,Junyoung Seo,Minseop Kwak,Jin-Hwa Kim,Seungryong Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CAMEO是一种通过几何对应关系直接监督注意力图的训练技术，显著提升多视角扩散模型的训练效率和生成质量，减少一半训练迭代次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多视角扩散模型虽然能实现视角一致的新视角合成，但其保持视角一致性的机制尚不明确。研究发现这些模型的注意力图能学习几何对应关系，但这种对应关系在大视角变化下不完整且准确性下降，需要改进。

Method: 提出CAMEO训练技术，直接使用几何对应关系监督注意力图。关键发现是只需监督单个注意力层就能引导模型学习精确对应关系，从而保留参考图像的几何结构，加速收敛。

Result: CAMEO将收敛所需的训练迭代次数减少了一半，同时在相同迭代次数下实现了更优的新视角合成性能。该方法模型无关，可应用于任何多视角扩散模型。

Conclusion: CAMEO通过直接监督注意力图的几何对应关系，有效提升了多视角扩散模型的训练效率和生成质量，为理解这类模型的工作原理提供了新见解，并提供了实用的改进方案。

Abstract: Multi-view diffusion models have recently emerged as a powerful paradigm for novel view synthesis, yet the underlying mechanism that enables their view-consistency remains unclear. In this work, we first verify that the attention maps of these models acquire geometric correspondence throughout training, attending to the geometrically corresponding regions across reference and target views for view-consistent generation. However, this correspondence signal remains incomplete, with its accuracy degrading under large viewpoint changes. Building on these findings, we introduce CAMEO, a simple yet effective training technique that directly supervises attention maps using geometric correspondence to enhance both the training efficiency and generation quality of multi-view diffusion models. Notably, supervising a single attention layer is sufficient to guide the model toward learning precise correspondences, thereby preserving the geometry and structure of reference images, accelerating convergence, and improving novel view synthesis performance. CAMEO reduces the number of training iterations required for convergence by half while achieving superior performance at the same iteration counts. We further demonstrate that CAMEO is model-agnostic and can be applied to any multi-view diffusion model.

中文标题: CAMEO：用于多视角扩散模型的对应注意力对齐

中文摘要: 多视角扩散模型最近已成为新颖视角合成的强大范式，然而使其保持视角一致性的底层机制仍不明确。在本工作中，我们首先验证了这些模型的注意力图在整个训练过程中获取了几何对应关系，能够关注参考视角和目标视角之间几何对应的区域以实现视角一致的生成。然而，这种对应信号仍然不完整，在大视角变化下其准确性会下降。基于这些发现，我们引入了CAMEO，这是一种简单而有效的训练技术，直接使用几何对应关系来监督注意力图，以增强多视角扩散模型的训练效率和生成质量。值得注意的是，监督单个注意力层就足以引导模型学习精确的对应关系，从而保留参考图像的几何结构和形状，加速收敛，并提高新颖视角合成性能。CAMEO将收敛所需的训练迭代次数减少了一半，同时在相同迭代次数下实现了更优的性能。我们进一步证明CAMEO是模型无关的，可以应用于任何多视角扩散模型。

</details>


### [93] [MagicQuillV2: Precise and Interactive Image Editing with Layered Visual Cues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.03046)
*Zichen Liu,Yue Yu,Hao Ouyang,Qiuyu Wang,Shuailei Ma,Ka Leong Cheng,Wen Wang,Qingyan Bai,Yuxuan Zhang,Yanhong Zeng,Yixuan Li,Xing Zhu,Yujun Shen,Qifeng Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MagicQuillV2提出分层组合范式，将图像编辑意图分解为内容、空间、结构和颜色四个可控视觉线索层，解决扩散模型语义能力与精细控制之间的差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散变换器使用单一整体提示，无法区分用户对内容、位置和外观的不同意图，导致生成控制粒度不足。

Method: 1) 用于上下文感知内容集成的专用数据生成流水线；2) 处理所有视觉线索的统一控制模块；3) 用于精确局部编辑（包括对象移除）的微调空间分支。

Result: 广泛实验验证了分层方法有效解决了用户意图差距，为创作者提供了直接、直观的生成过程控制。

Conclusion: MagicQuillV2通过分层组合范式在扩散模型的语义能力和传统图形软件的精细控制之间架起了桥梁。

Abstract: We propose MagicQuill V2, a novel system that introduces a \textbf{layered composition} paradigm to generative image editing, bridging the gap between the semantic power of diffusion models and the granular control of traditional graphics software. While diffusion transformers excel at holistic generation, their use of singular, monolithic prompts fails to disentangle distinct user intentions for content, position, and appearance. To overcome this, our method deconstructs creative intent into a stack of controllable visual cues: a content layer for what to create, a spatial layer for where to place it, a structural layer for how it is shaped, and a color layer for its palette. Our technical contributions include a specialized data generation pipeline for context-aware content integration, a unified control module to process all visual cues, and a fine-tuned spatial branch for precise local editing, including object removal. Extensive experiments validate that this layered approach effectively resolves the user intention gap, granting creators direct, intuitive control over the generative process.

中文标题: MagicQuillV2：基于分层视觉线索的精确交互式图像编辑

中文摘要: 我们提出了MagicQuill V2，这是一个新颖的系统，将分层组合范式引入生成式图像编辑，弥合了扩散模型的语义能力与传统图形软件的精细控制之间的差距。虽然扩散变换器在全景生成方面表现出色，但它们使用单一的整体提示无法区分用户对内容、位置和外观的不同意图。为了克服这一问题，我们的方法将创作意图解构为一系列可控的视觉线索：内容层（创建什么）、空间层（放置在哪里）、结构层（如何塑造）和颜色层（调色板）。我们的技术贡献包括：用于上下文感知内容集成的专用数据生成流水线，处理所有视觉线索的统一控制模块，以及用于精确局部编辑（包括对象移除）的微调空间分支。大量实验验证了这种分层方法有效解决了用户意图差距，为创作者提供了直接、直观的生成过程控制。

</details>

### [94] [Story2MIDI: Emotionally Aligned Music Generation from Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02192)

Method: 1. 构建Story2MIDI数据集：合并现有的文本情感分析和音乐情感分类数据集，创建文本片段和音乐片段的情感配对数据。2. 开发基于Transformer的序列到序列模型，学习文本和音乐之间的情感对应关系。3. 使用该模型从文本生成情感对齐的MIDI音乐。

Despite the small scale of our dataset and limited computational resources, our results indicate that our model effectively learns emotion-relevant features in music and incorporates them into its generation process, producing samples with diverse emotional responses. We evaluate the generated outputs using objective musical metrics and a human listening study, confirming the model's ability to capture intended emotional cues.

中文标题: Story2MIDI：基于文本的情感对齐音乐生成

*Ankur Gupta,Anshul Rai,Archit Bansal,Vipul Arora*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 提出一种基于深度学习的交互式持续学习框架，用于人声分离，允许用户通过标记误报区域来微调模型，以适应新歌曲。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人声分离模型缺乏用户交互能力，无法适应现实场景中音乐风格和乐器的多样性变化。需要一种允许用户参与模型优化的方法。

Method: 使用U-Net基础模型从频谱图中生成人声分离掩码，然后通过人机交互环节让用户标记误报区域（本应是静音的部分），并提出两种持续学习算法。

In this paper, we present a deep learning-based interactive continual learning framework for singing voice separation that allows users to fine-tune the vocal separation model to conform it to new target songs. ### [96] [Exploring Definitions of Quality and Diversity in Sonic Measurement Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02783)
*Björn Þór Jónsson,Çağrı Erdem,Stefano Fasciani,Kyrre Glette*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 该研究探索了在声音测量空间中自动定义质量与多样性的方法，使用无监督降维技术（PCA和自编码器）为QD进化算法动态配置行为空间，相比手工设计的方法能获得更大的多样性且避免专家偏见。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字声音合成提供了探索包含数百万配置的巨大参数空间的机会。质量多样性（QD）进化算法为利用这一潜力提供了有前景的方法，但其成功依赖于适当的声音特征表示。现有的QD方法主要使用手工设计的描述符或有监督分类器，可能引入意外的探索偏见并将发现限制在熟悉的声音区域。

Method: 本研究调查了无监督降维方法，用于在QD搜索期间自动定义和动态重新配置声音行为空间。应用主成分分析（PCA）和自编码器将高维音频特征投影到MAP-Elites的结构化网格上，通过定期重新训练模型实现动态重新配置。

Result: 在两个实验场景中的比较显示，自动方法比手工设计的行为空间实现了显著更大的多样性，同时避免了专家强加的偏见。动态行为空间重新配置保持了进化压力并防止停滞，其中PCA在降维技术中证明最为有效。

Conclusion: 这些结果有助于构建能够探索巨大参数空间而无需人工干预或有监督训练约束的自动化声音发现系统。

Abstract: Digital sound synthesis presents the opportunity to explore vast parameter spaces containing millions of configurations. Quality diversity (QD) evolutionary algorithms offer a promising approach to harness this potential, yet their success hinges on appropriate sonic feature representations. Existing QD methods predominantly employ handcrafted descriptors or supervised classifiers, potentially introducing unintended exploration biases and constraining discovery to familiar sonic regions. This work investigates unsupervised dimensionality reduction methods for automatically defining and dynamically reconfiguring sonic behaviour spaces during QD search. We apply Principal Component Analysis (PCA) and autoencoders to project high-dimensional audio features onto structured grids for MAP-Elites, implementing dynamic reconfiguration through model retraining at regular intervals. Comparison across two experimental scenarios shows that automatic approaches achieve significantly greater diversity than handcrafted behaviour spaces while avoiding expert-imposed biases. Dynamic behaviour-space reconfiguration maintains evolutionary pressure and prevents stagnation, with PCA proving most effective among the dimensionality reduction techniques. These results contribute to automated sonic discovery systems capable of exploring vast parameter spaces without manual intervention or supervised training constraints.

中文标题: 探索声音测量空间中质量与多样性的定义

中文摘要: 数字声音合成为探索包含数百万配置的巨大参数空间提供了机会。质量多样性（QD）进化算法为利用这一潜力提供了有前景的方法，但其成功依赖于适当的声音特征表示。现有的QD方法主要使用手工设计的描述符或有监督分类器，可能引入意外的探索偏见并将发现限制在熟悉的声音区域。本研究调查了无监督降维方法，用于在QD搜索期间自动定义和动态重新配置声音行为空间。我们应用主成分分析（PCA）和自编码器将高维音频特征投影到MAP-Elites的结构化网格上，通过定期重新训练模型实现动态重新配置。在两个实验场景中的比较显示，自动方法比手工设计的行为空间实现了显著更大的多样性，同时避免了专家强加的偏见。动态行为空间重新配置保持了进化压力并防止停滞，其中PCA在降维技术中证明最为有效。这些结果有助于构建能够探索巨大参数空间而无需人工干预或有监督训练约束的自动化声音发现系统。

</details>


### [97] [Generative Multi-modal Feedback for Singing Voice Synthesis Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02523)
*Xueyan Li,Yuxin Wang,Mengjie Jiang,Qingzi Zhu,Jiang Zhang,Zoey Kim,Yazhe Niu*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 提出了一个生成式多模态反馈框架，用于歌声合成评估，通过音频-语言模型生成文本和音频评论，解决传统单一数值评分方法的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着歌声合成技术的进步，需要更可靠的评估方法。现有方法依赖单一数值评分，难以捕捉音乐表达的多个维度（如乐句、表现力），且需要昂贵的人工标注，限制了可解释性和泛化能力。

Method: 提出了一个生成式反馈框架，利用音频-语言模型生成多维度的语言和音频评论。模型在混合数据集上微调，该数据集结合了人类音乐反应和来自多模态大语言模型的合成评论，以增强多样性和语言丰富性。

Result: 定量实验验证了所提数据集和训练策略的有效性。该框架能够产生音乐准确且可解释的评估，适用于指导生成模型的改进。

Conclusion: 提出的生成式多模态反馈框架为歌声合成评估提供了更全面、可解释的解决方案，能够捕捉传统方法难以评估的音乐表达维度，有助于推动歌声合成技术的进一步发展。

Abstract: Singing voice synthesis (SVS) has advanced significantly, enabling models to generate vocals with accurate pitch and consistent style. As these capabilities improve, the need for reliable evaluation and optimization becomes increasingly critical. However, current methods like reward systems often rely on single numerical scores, struggle to capture various dimensions such as phrasing or expressiveness, and require costly annotations, limiting interpretability and generalization. To address these issues, we propose a generative feedback (i.e., reward model) framework that provides multi-dimensional language and audio feedback for SVS assessment. Our approach leverages an audio-language model to generate text and audio critiques-covering aspects such as melody, content, and auditory quality. The model is fine-tuned on a hybrid dataset combining human music reactions and synthetic critiques from a MLLMs, enhancing diversity and linguistic richness. Quantitative experiments validate the effectiveness of the proposed dataset and training strategy, demonstrating that the framework produces musically accurate and interpretable evaluations suitable for guiding generative model improvement. The code is at [https://github.com/opendilab/VocalCritic](https://github.com/opendilab/VocalCritic)

中文标题: 生成式多模态反馈在歌声合成评估中的应用

中文摘要: 歌声合成技术已取得显著进展，能够生成具有准确音高和一致风格的歌声。随着这些能力的提升，对可靠评估和优化的需求变得日益重要。然而，当前的奖励系统等方法通常依赖单一数值评分，难以捕捉诸如乐句表达或表现力等多个维度，且需要昂贵的标注，限制了可解释性和泛化能力。为解决这些问题，我们提出了一个生成式反馈（即奖励模型）框架，为SVS评估提供多维度的语言和音频反馈。我们的方法利用音频-语言模型生成文本和音频评论，涵盖旋律、内容和听觉质量等方面。该模型在结合人类音乐反应和来自MLLMs的合成评论的混合数据集上进行微调，增强了多样性和语言丰富性。定量实验验证了所提数据集和训练策略的有效性，表明该框架能够产生音乐准确且可解释的评估，适用于指导生成模型的改进。代码位于[https://github.com/opendilab/VocalCritic](https://github.com/opendilab/VocalCritic)

### [98] [Pianist Transformer: Towards Expressive Piano Performance Rendering via Scalable Self-Supervised Pre-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02652)
*Hong-Jie You,Jie-Jing Shao,Xiao-Wen Yang,Lin-Han Jia,Lan-Zhe Guo,Yu-Feng Li*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: Pianist Transformer是一个通过自监督预训练实现钢琴表现力演奏渲染的模型，使用统一MIDI表示、非对称架构、大规模预训练，在客观指标和主观评分上达到最先进水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有表现力音乐演奏渲染方法依赖小规模标注数据的监督学习，限制了数据和模型规模的扩展，尽管存在大量未标注音乐数据。需要解决这一差距以实现可扩展的表现力演奏合成。

Method: 1) 统一MIDI数据表示学习音乐结构和表现力的共享原理；2) 高效非对称架构支持更长上下文和更快推理；3) 自监督预训练流程使用100亿token和1.35亿参数模型；4) 实现最先进的性能模型。

Result: 模型在客观指标上表现强劲，主观评分达到人类水平，为音乐领域实现人类级表现力合成建立了可扩展路径。

Conclusion: Pianist Transformer通过自监督预训练解决了表现力钢琴演奏渲染的可扩展性问题，为音乐领域实现人类级表现力合成提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Existing methods for expressive music performance rendering rely on supervised learning over small labeled datasets, which limits scaling of both data volume and model size, despite the availability of vast unlabeled music, as in vision and language. To address this gap, we introduce Pianist Transformer, with four key contributions: 1) a unified Musical Instrument Digital Interface (MIDI) data representation for learning the shared principles of musical structure and expression without explicit annotation; 2) an efficient asymmetric architecture, enabling longer contexts and faster inference without sacrificing rendering quality; 3) a self-supervised pre-training pipeline with 10B tokens and 135M-parameter model, unlocking data and model scaling advantages for expressive performance rendering; 4) a state-of-the-art performance model, which achieves strong objective metrics and human-level subjective ratings. Overall, Pianist Transformer establishes a scalable path toward human-like performance synthesis in the music domain.

中文标题: Pianist Transformer：通过可扩展自监督预训练实现表现力钢琴演奏渲染

中文摘要: 现有的表现力音乐演奏渲染方法依赖于小规模标注数据集的监督学习，这限制了数据量和模型规模的扩展，尽管存在大量未标注音乐数据，就像视觉和语言领域一样。为解决这一差距，我们引入了Pianist Transformer，具有四个关键贡献：1) 统一的MIDI数据表示，用于学习音乐结构和表现力的共享原理而无需显式标注；2) 高效的非对称架构，支持更长上下文和更快推理而不牺牲渲染质量；3) 包含100亿token和1.35亿参数模型的自监督预训练流程，解锁了表现力演奏渲染的数据和模型扩展优势；4) 最先进的性能模型，在客观指标和人类级主观评分上表现强劲。总体而言，Pianist Transformer为音乐领域实现人类级表现力合成建立了可扩展路径。

# cs.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [99] [On the Complexity of Signed Roman Domination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02083)
*Sangam Balchandar Reddy*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了有符号罗马支配问题的计算复杂性，证明了该问题在分裂图上也是NP完全的，在参数化复杂性方面证明了多个硬度结果，并给出了一个FPT算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有符号罗马支配问题是图论中的一个重要优化问题，之前已知在二分图和平面图上是NP完全的。本文旨在进一步探索该问题的计算复杂性边界，特别是在分裂图上的复杂性，以及在参数化复杂性框架下的分类。

Method: 采用复杂性理论分析方法，包括NP完全性证明、参数化复杂性分析（W[1]-hard和W[2]-hard证明）、FPT算法设计以及核复杂性分析。

Result: 1. 证明了有符号罗马支配问题在分裂图上是NP完全的；2. 证明了该问题在权重参数化下是W[2]-难的（即使在二分图上）；3. 证明了该问题在反馈顶点集数参数化下是W[1]-难的；4. 提出了在邻域多样性和顶点覆盖数参数化下的FPT算法；5. 证明了该问题在顶点覆盖数参数化下不允许多项式核（除非coNP ⊆ NP/poly）。

Conclusion: 有符号罗马支配问题具有丰富的复杂性结构：在分裂图上仍然是NP完全的，在多个参数化下表现出不同的复杂性行为，既有硬度结果也有可处理性结果，为理解该问题的计算边界提供了全面视角。

Abstract: Given a graph $G = (V, E)$, a signed Roman dominating function is a function $f: V \rightarrow \{-1, 1, 2\}$ such that for every vertex $u \in V$: $\sum_{v \in N[u]} f(v) \geq 1$ and for every vertex $u \in V$ with $f(u) = -1$, there exists a vertex $v \in N(u)$ with $f(v) = 2$. The weight of a signed Roman dominating function $f$ is $\sum_{u \in V} f(u)$. The objective of \srd{} (SRD) problem is to compute a signed Roman dominating function with minimum weight. The problem is known to be NP-complete even when restricted to bipartite graphs and planar graphs. In this paper, we advance the complexity study by showing that the problem remains NP-complete on split graphs. In the realm of parameterized complexity, we prove that the problem is W[2]-hard parameterized by weight, even on bipartite graphs. We further show that the problem is W[1]-hard parameterized by feedback vertex set number (and hence also when parameterized by treewidth or clique-width). On the positive side, we present an FPT algorithm parameterized by neighbourhood diversity (and by vertex cover number). Finally, we complement this result by proving that the problem does not admit a polynomial kernel parameterized by vertex cover number unless coNP $\subseteq$ NP/poly.

中文标题: 关于有符号罗马支配问题的复杂性分析

中文摘要: 给定一个图$G = (V, E)$，有符号罗马支配函数是一个函数$f: V \rightarrow \{-1, 1, 2\}$，满足对于每个顶点$u \in V$：$\sum_{v \in N[u]} f(v) \geq 1$，并且对于每个满足$f(u) = -1$的顶点$u \in V$，存在一个顶点$v \in N(u)$满足$f(v) = 2$。有符号罗马支配函数$f$的权重为$\sum_{u \in V} f(u)$。SRD问题的目标是计算具有最小权重的有符号罗马支配函数。已知该问题即使在二分图和平面图上也是NP完全的。本文通过证明该问题在分裂图上仍然是NP完全的，推进了复杂性研究。在参数化复杂性领域，我们证明了该问题在权重参数化下是W[2]-难的，即使在二分图上也是如此。我们进一步证明了该问题在反馈顶点集数参数化下是W[1]-难的（因此在树宽或团宽参数化下也是如此）。在积极方面，我们提出了一个在邻域多样性（以及顶点覆盖数）参数化下的FPT算法。最后，我们通过证明除非coNP $\subseteq$ NP/poly，否则该问题在顶点覆盖数参数化下不允许多项式核，从而补充了这一结果。

</details>


### [100] [Markov Chains Approximate Message Passing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02384)
*Amit Rajaraman,David X. Wu*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文建立了马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛算法（特别是Glauber动力学）与近似消息传递（AMP）在尖峰Wigner推断问题中的理论联系，证明了RGD辅助马尔可夫链能够达到贝叶斯最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛算法在实践中表现出接近最优的贝叶斯推断性能，但缺乏严格的理论支持。本文旨在为Glauber动力学在尖峰Wigner推断问题中的优异表现提供理论依据，并将其与已知最优的AMP算法联系起来。

Method: 通过分析一个称为受限高斯动力学（RGD）的辅助马尔可夫链，将其简化为与AMP迭代演化相似的一维递归。从热启动条件出发，分析RGD在相关性空间中的收敛行为，并与AMP的性能进行对比。

Result: 1. RGD可以简化为有效的一维递归，与AMP迭代演化一致
2. 从热启动开始，RGD快速收敛到固定点，能够恢复贝叶斯最优性能
3. 在SK模型混合结果的条件下，恢复了非平凡推断的相变

Conclusion: 本文为马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛算法在贝叶斯推断中的优异表现提供了理论支持，建立了Glauber动力学与AMP之间的严格联系，证明了在尖峰Wigner问题中，适当的马尔可夫链方法能够达到贝叶斯最优性能。

Abstract: Markov chain Monte Carlo algorithms have long been observed to obtain near-optimal performance in various Bayesian inference settings. However, developing a supporting theory that make these studies rigorous has proved challenging.
  In this paper, we study the classical spiked Wigner inference problem, where one aims to recover a planted Boolean spike from a noisy matrix measurement. We relate the recovery performance of Glauber dynamics on the annealed posterior to the performance of Approximate Message Passing (AMP), which is known to achieve Bayes-optimal performance. Our main results rely on the analysis of an auxiliary Markov chain called restricted Gaussian dynamics (RGD). Concretely, we establish the following results:
  1. RGD can be reduced to an effective one-dimensional recursion which mirrors the evolution of the AMP iterates.
  2. From a warm start, RGD rapidly converges to a fixed point in correlation space, which recovers Bayes-optimal performance when run on the posterior.
  3. Conditioned on widely believed mixing results for the SK model, we recover the phase transition for non-trivial inference.

中文标题: 马尔可夫链近似消息传递

中文摘要: 马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛算法长期以来在各种贝叶斯推断设置中被观察到能够获得接近最优的性能。然而，建立一个支持这些研究的严格理论一直具有挑战性。

在本文中，我们研究了经典的尖峰Wigner推断问题，其中目标是从噪声矩阵测量中恢复一个植入的布尔尖峰。我们将退火后验上的Glauber动力学的恢复性能与近似消息传递（AMP）的性能联系起来，已知AMP能够实现贝叶斯最优性能。我们的主要结果依赖于对一个称为受限高斯动力学（RGD）的辅助马尔可夫链的分析。具体来说，我们建立了以下结果：
1. RGD可以简化为一个有效的一维递归，该递归反映了AMP迭代的演化。
2. 从热启动开始，RGD在相关性空间中快速收敛到一个固定点，当在后验上运行时，该固定点能够恢复贝叶斯最优性能。
3. 基于广泛相信的SK模型混合结果的条件，我们恢复了非平凡推断的相变。

### [101] [New Bounds for Circular Trace Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02412)
*Arnav Burudgunte,Paul Valiant,Hongao Wang*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文改进了圆形轨迹重建问题的下界至$\tildeΩ(n^5)$，并证明对于恒定稀疏字符串，$\tilde{O}(n^6)$个轨迹足以重建，表明未来研究应关注非恒定稀疏字符串。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨迹重建问题在已知上界和下界之间存在指数级差距，需要新的方法来缩小这一差距。圆形轨迹重建作为该问题的一个变体，通过引入随机循环移位，可能揭示新的理论见解。

Method: 使用傅里叶技术分析循环删除信道下的轨迹重建，特别关注稀疏字符串的情况。通过构造两个具有恒定数量非零比特的稀疏字符串，证明其轨迹的不可区分性，从而建立下界。

Result: 1. 证明了圆形轨迹重建的改进下界$\tildeΩ(n^5)$；2. 证明了对于任何恒定稀疏字符串，$\tilde{O}(n^6)$个轨迹足以在循环删除信道中重建；3. 揭示了稀疏字符串与一般字符串在重建复杂度上的显著差异。

Conclusion: 圆形轨迹重建对于恒定稀疏字符串具有多项式复杂度的上界，而一般字符串需要指数级轨迹。这表明未来的算法设计或下界证明必须专注于非恒定稀疏字符串，才能解决轨迹重建问题的核心挑战。

Abstract: The ''trace reconstruction'' problem asks, given an unknown binary string $x$ and a channel that repeatedly returns ''traces'' of $x$ with each bit randomly deleted with some probability $p$, how many traces are needed to recover $x$? There is an exponential gap between the best known upper and lower bounds for this problem. Many variants of the model have been introduced in hopes of motivating or revealing new approaches to narrow this gap. We study the variant of circular trace reconstruction introduced by Narayanan and Ren (ITCS 2021), in which traces undergo a random cyclic shift in addition to random deletions.
  We show an improved lower bound of $\tildeΩ(n^5)$ for circular trace reconstruction. This contrasts with the (previously) best known lower bounds of $\tildeΩ(n^3)$ in the circular case and $\tildeΩ(n^{3/2})$ in the linear case. Our bound shows the indistinguishability of traces from two sparse strings $x,y$ that each have a constant number of nonzeros. Can this technique be extended significantly? How hard is it to reconstruct a sparse string $x$ under a cyclic deletion channel? We resolve these questions by showing, using Fourier techniques, that $\tilde{O}(n^6)$ traces suffice for reconstructing any constant-sparse string in a circular deletion channel, in contrast to the upper bound of $\exp(\tilde{O}(n^{1/3}))$ for general strings in the circular deletion channel. This shows that new algorithms or new lower bounds must focus on non-constant-sparse strings.

中文标题: 圆形轨迹重建的新边界

中文摘要: "轨迹重建"问题询问：给定一个未知的二进制字符串$x$和一个信道，该信道重复返回$x$的"轨迹"，其中每个比特以概率$p$随机删除，需要多少轨迹才能恢复$x$？这个问题的最佳已知上界和下界之间存在指数级差距。为了激励或揭示缩小这一差距的新方法，已经引入了该模型的许多变体。我们研究了Narayanan和Ren（ITCS 2021）引入的圆形轨迹重建变体，其中轨迹除了随机删除外还经历随机循环移位。

我们展示了圆形轨迹重建的改进下界$\tildeΩ(n^5)$。这与先前已知的圆形情况下的$\tildeΩ(n^3)$下界和线性情况下的$\tildeΩ(n^{3/2})$下界形成对比。我们的边界显示了来自两个稀疏字符串$x,y$的轨迹的不可区分性，每个字符串都有恒定数量的非零比特。这种技术能否显著扩展？在循环删除信道下重建稀疏字符串$x$有多难？我们通过使用傅里叶技术表明，$\tilde{O}(n^6)$个轨迹足以在循环删除信道中重建任何恒定稀疏字符串，这与圆形删除信道中一般字符串的$\exp(\tilde{O}(n^{1/3}))$上界形成对比。这表明新算法或新下界必须专注于非恒定稀疏字符串。

</details>


### [102] [Approximation schemes for covering and packing mixed-integer programs with a fixed number of constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02571)
*Kobe Grobben,Phablo F. S. Moura,Hande Yaman*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该论文提出了针对具有固定约束数量的覆盖和包装混合整数规划问题的近似方案，包括多项式时间近似方案（PTAS）、完全多项式时间近似方案（FPTAS）和近似线性规划公式，改进了现有算法性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合整数线性规划在组合优化中广泛应用，但许多经典覆盖问题（如多维背包、设施选址、供应商选择）缺乏高效的近似算法。现有算法如2-近似算法存在改进空间，需要为更一般的覆盖混合整数规划类设计近似方案。

Method: 首先分析相关多面体顶点性质，利用这些性质将问题分解为每个维度具有单个连续变量的多维背包覆盖问题实例。基于分解设计固定约束数问题的多项式时间近似方案（PTAS），针对单约束情况设计完全多项式时间近似方案（FPTAS）和近似线性规划公式，并对变量具有相同上下界的情况提出完美紧凑公式。

Result: 提出了首个针对一般覆盖混合整数规划类的近似方案，包括PTAS、FPTAS和近似线性规划公式。对于单约束情况，改进了先前背包覆盖问题的最佳2-近似算法。同时推导了包装和分配变体的类似结果。

Conclusion: 该研究为具有固定约束数量的覆盖和包装混合整数规划问题提供了系统的近似算法框架，填补了该领域的研究空白，并为多维背包、设施选址等经典问题提供了更高效的近似解决方案。

Abstract: This paper presents an algorithmic study of a class of covering mixed-integer linear programming problems which encompasses classic cover problems, including multidimensional knapsack, facility location and supplier selection problems. We first show some properties of the vertices of the associated polytope, which are then used to decompose the problem into instances of the multidimensional knapsack cover problem with a single continuous variable per dimension. The proposed decomposition is used to design a polynomial-time approximation scheme for the problem with a fixed number of constraints. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first approximation scheme for such a general class of covering mixed-integer programs. Moreover, we design a fully polynomial-time approximation scheme and an approximate linear programming formulation for the case with a single constraint. These results improve upon the previously best-known 2-approximation algorithm for the knapsack cover problem with a single continuous variable. Finally, we show a perfect compact formulation for the case where all variables have the same lower and upper bounds. Analogous results are derived for the packing and assignment variants of the problem.

中文标题: 具有固定约束数量的覆盖和包装混合整数规划的近似方案

中文摘要: 本文对一类覆盖混合整数线性规划问题进行了算法研究，该类问题涵盖了经典覆盖问题，包括多维背包、设施选址和供应商选择问题。我们首先展示了相关多面体顶点的性质，然后利用这些性质将问题分解为每个维度具有单个连续变量的多维背包覆盖问题实例。所提出的分解用于设计固定约束数问题的多项式时间近似方案。据我们所知，这是首个针对如此一般的覆盖混合整数规划类的近似方案。此外，我们为单约束情况设计了完全多项式时间近似方案和近似线性规划公式。这些结果改进了先前单连续变量背包覆盖问题的最佳2-近似算法。最后，我们展示了所有变量具有相同上下界情况的完美紧凑公式。类似的结果也推导出了问题的包装和分配变体。

### [103] [The Support of Bin Packing is Exponential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02758)
*Klaus Jansen,Lis Pirotton,Malte Tutas*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 证明了装箱问题支持度的指数级下界为2^Ω(d)，与已知上界2^d匹配，并开发了新的整数线性规划聚合技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究装箱问题中不同填充方式箱子数量的下界，这对理解问题复杂度和算法效率有重要意义。现有上界为2^d，但下界未知，需要填补这一理论空白。

Method: 开发了一种新的整数线性规划聚合技术，能够将具有多个等式约束的ILP聚合为等价的单约束ILP，同时整合变量的上界约束。

Result: 证明了装箱问题支持度的下界为2^Ω(d)，与已知上界2^d在常数因子内匹配，建立了紧的指数级界限。

Conclusion: 装箱问题的支持度呈指数级增长，这一结果对多个装箱算法的时间复杂度有直接影响，同时提出的ILP聚合技术具有更广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Consider the classical Bin Packing problem with $d$ different item sizes $s_i$ and amounts of items $a_i.$ The support of a Bin Packing solution is the number of differently filled bins. In this work, we show that the lower bound on the support of this problem is $2^{Ω(d)}$. Our lower bound matches the upper bound of $2^d$ given by Eisenbrand and Shmonin [Oper.Research Letters '06] up to a constant factor. This result has direct implications for the time complexity of several Bin Packing algorithms, such as Goemans and Rothvoss [SODA '14], Jansen and Klein [SODA '17] and Jansen and Solis-Oba [IPCO '10]. To achieve our main result, we develop a technique to aggregate equality constrained ILPs with many constraints into an equivalent ILP with one constraint. Our technique contrasts existing aggregation techniques as we manage to integrate upper bounds on variables into the resulting constraint. We believe this technique can be useful for solving general ILPs or the $d$-dimensional knapsack problem.

中文标题: 装箱问题支持度的指数级下界

中文摘要: 考虑具有$d$种不同物品尺寸$s_i$和数量$a_i$的经典装箱问题。装箱方案的支持度是指不同填充方式的箱子数量。在这项工作中，我们证明了该问题支持度的下界为$2^{Ω(d)}$。我们的下界与Eisenbrand和Shmonin [Oper.Research Letters '06]给出的$2^d$上界在常数因子内匹配。这一结果对多种装箱算法的时间复杂度有直接影响，如Goemans和Rothvoss [SODA '14]、Jansen和Klein [SODA '17]以及Jansen和Solis-Oba [IPCO '10]。为实现主要结果，我们开发了一种将具有多个约束的等式约束整数线性规划聚合为等价单约束整数线性规划的技术。我们的技术与现有聚合技术形成对比，因为我们成功地将变量的上界整合到结果约束中。我们相信这项技术对于解决一般整数线性规划或$d$维背包问题可能有用。

### [104] [Young Children's Anthropomorphism of AI Chatbots and the Role of Parent Co-Presence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02179)
*Pilyoung Kim,Jenna H. Chin,Yun Xie,Nolan Brady,Tom Yeh,Sujin Yang*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: Artificial Intelligence (AI) chatbots powered by a large language model (LLM) are entering young children's learning and play, yet little is known about how young children construe these agents or how such construals relate to engagement. We examined anthropomorphism of a social AI chatbot during collaborative storytelling and asked how children's attributions related to their behavior and prefrontal activation. Children at ages 5-6 (N = 23) completed three storytelling sessions: interacting with (1) an AI chatbot only, (2) a parent only, and (3) the AI and a parent together. After the sessions, children completed an interview assessing anthropomorphism toward both the AI chatbot and the parent. Behavioral engagement was indexed by the conversational turn count (CTC) ratio, and concurrent fNIRS measured oxygenated hemoglobin in bilateral vmPFC and dmPFC regions. Children reported higher anthropomorphism for parents than for the AI chatbot overall, although AI ratings were relatively high for perceptive abilities and epistemic states. Anthropomorphism was not associated with CTC. In the right dmPFC, higher perceptive scores were associated with greater activation during the AI-only condition and with lower activation during the AI+Parent condition. Exploratory analyses indicated that higher dmPFC activation during the AI-only condition correlated with higher end-of-session "scared" mood ratings. Findings suggest that stronger perceptive anthropomorphism can be associated with greater brain activation related to interpreting the AI's mental states, whereas parent co-presence may help some children interpret and regulate novel AI interactions. These results may have design implications for encouraging parent-AI co-use in early childhood.

### [105] [DepthScape: Authoring 2.5D Designs via Depth Estimation, Semantic Understanding, and Geometry Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02263)
*Xia Su,Cuong Nguyen,Matheus A. Gadelha,Jon E. Froehlich*

TL;DR: DepthScape是一个AI辅助的2.5D设计系统，通过深度估计、语义理解和几何提取，简化了在2D图像中创建3D深度效果的过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 2.5D效果（如遮挡和透视缩短）能增强视觉动态和真实感，但创建这些效果仍然具有挑战性且劳动密集，因为深度感知的复杂性。

Method: DepthScape使用单目深度重建将图像转换为3D重建，视觉内容自动实现逼真的遮挡和透视缩短。系统还使用视觉语言模型分析源图像并提取关键视觉组件作为内容锚点，通过2D视口简化3D放置。

Result: 通过9名不同设计背景参与者的评估确认了创作流程的有效性。在100张专业库存图像上测试了鲁棒性，专家评估确认了DepthScape结果的质量。

Conclusion: DepthScape是一个有效的人机协作系统，通过深度估计、语义理解和几何提取，显著简化了2.5D效果的创作过程。

Abstract: 2.5D effects, such as occlusion and perspective foreshortening, enhance visual dynamics and realism by incorporating 3D depth cues into 2D designs. However, creating such effects remains challenging and labor-intensive due to the complexity of depth perception. We introduce DepthScape, a human-AI collaborative system that facilitates 2.5D effect creation by directly placing design elements into 3D reconstructions. Using monocular depth reconstruction, DepthScape transforms images into 3D reconstructions where visual contents are placed to automatically achieve realistic occlusion and perspective foreshortening. To further simplify 3D placement through a 2D viewport, DepthScape uses a vision-language model to analyze source images and extract key visual components as content anchors for direct manipulation editing. We evaluate DepthScape with nine participants of varying design backgrounds, confirming the effectiveness of our creation pipeline. We also test on 100 professional stock images to assess robustness, and conduct an expert evaluation that confirms the quality of DepthScape's results.

### [106] [Understanding Down Syndrome Stereotypes in LLM-Based Personas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02275)
*Chantelle Wu,Peinan Wang,Nafi Nibras,Meida Li,Dajun Yuan,Zhixiao Wang,Jiahuan He,Mona Ali,Mirjana Prpa*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 该研究分析了LLM生成唐氏综合征人物角色时的刻板印象问题，开发了Persona-L系统并集成了刻板印象检测功能，通过访谈揭示了训练数据、界面设计和LLM输出语气中潜在的刻板印象风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人物角色创建方法往往导致对唐氏综合征患者的过度简化或刻板印象描述，需要开发能够检测和避免刻板印象的系统，以更准确地反映唐氏综合征患者的多样性和真实生活经历。

Method: 开发了Persona-L系统，结合大型语言模型和检索增强生成技术，并集成了刻板印象检测功能。通过访谈10名护理人员和医疗专业人员，分析LLM在内容和表达方式上可能出现的唐氏综合征刻板印象，以及界面设计的影响。

Result: 研究发现刻板印象定义存在挑战，揭示了训练数据、界面设计和LLM输出语气中潜在的刻板印象出现。访谈显示需要参与式方法来捕捉唐氏综合征患者生活经历的异质性。

Conclusion: LLM在生成唐氏综合征人物角色时容易产生刻板印象，需要采用参与式设计方法，考虑训练数据、界面设计和输出语气等多方面因素，以更准确地反映唐氏综合征患者的多样性。

Abstract: We present a case study of Persona-L, a system that leverages large language models (LLMs) and retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) to model personas of people with Down syndrome. Existing approaches to persona creation can often lead to oversimplified or stereotypical profiles of people with Down Syndrome. To that end, we built stereotype detection capabilities into Persona-L. Through interviews with caregivers and healthcare professionals (N=10), we examine how Down Syndrome stereotypes could manifest in both, content and delivery of LLMs, and interface design. Our findings show the challenges in stereotypes definition, and reveal the potential stereotype emergence from the training data, interface design, and the tone of LLM output. This highlights the need for participatory methods that capture the heterogeneity of lived experiences of people with Down Syndrome.

中文标题: 理解基于LLM的人物角色中的唐氏综合征刻板印象

中文摘要: 我们提出了Persona-L系统的案例研究，该系统利用大型语言模型和检索增强生成技术来建模唐氏综合征患者的人物角色。现有的人物角色创建方法往往导致对唐氏综合征患者的过度简化或刻板印象描述。为此，我们在Persona-L中构建了刻板印象检测功能。通过对护理人员和医疗专业人员的访谈，我们研究了唐氏综合征刻板印象如何在LLM的内容和表达方式以及界面设计中体现。我们的研究结果显示刻板印象定义存在挑战，并揭示了训练数据、界面设计和LLM输出语气中潜在的刻板印象出现。这突显了需要采用参与式方法来捕捉唐氏综合征患者生活经历的异质性。

</details>


### [107] [Artographer: a Curatorial Interface for Art Space Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02288)
*Shm Garanganao Almeda,John Joon Young Chung,Bjoern Hartmann,Sophia Liu,Brett Halperin,Yuwen Lu,Max Kreminski*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: Artographer是一个基于嵌入模型的艺术探索系统，通过可缩放的2D地图展示15,000+历史艺术品的相似性聚类，支持用户发现和关联艺术作品。研究通过20名参与者（包括9名艺术史学者）的探索行为分析，识别了不同的探索模式（跳跃、漫游、专注、重访）和空间艺术发现的价值（可见性、能动性、偶然性、摩擦）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI界面在艺术探索中往往模糊了作品之间的关系，而不是帮助用户探索这些关系。嵌入模型为通过空间交互发现和关联艺术品提供了新的机会，但需要设计能够支持这种探索的界面。

Method: 开发了Artographer系统，基于15,000+历史艺术品的嵌入模型相似性聚类构建可缩放的2D地图。通过20名参与者（包括9名艺术史学者）进行用户研究，分析他们在目标驱动任务和自由探索中的地图遍历行为，识别探索模式和价值。

Result: 观察到四种探索行为：跳跃（在不同区域间快速移动）、漫游（在相邻区域间缓慢移动）、专注（在特定区域深入探索）、重访（返回先前访问过的区域）。识别了空间艺术发现的四个核心价值：可见性（作品关系的可视化）、能动性（用户控制探索）、偶然性（意外发现）、摩擦（探索中的阻力）。

Conclusion: 空间地图应被视为策展界面的一种形式，这类系统选择和呈现艺术品。在设计更负责任的艺术策展AI系统时，应关注多元主义和能动性，支持用户发现和建立艺术品之间的关系。

Abstract: Relating a piece to previously established works is crucial in creating and engaging with art, but AI interfaces tend to obscure such relationships, rather than helping users explore them. Embedding models present new opportunities to support discovering and relating artwork through spatial interaction. We built Artographer, an art exploration system featuring a zoomable 2-D map, constructed from the similarity-clustered embeddings of 15,000+ historical artworks. Using Artographer as a probe to investigate spatial artwork exploration, we analyzed how 20 participants (including 9 art history scholars) traversed the map, during a goal-driven task and when freely exploring. We observe divergent and convergent exploration behaviors (Jumping, Wandering, Fixation, Revisiting) and identify values enacted by spatial art-finding (Visibility, Agency, Serendipity, Friction.) We situate spatial maps within a space of Curatorial Interfaces, systems that select and present artworks, and discuss centering pluralism and agency in the design of more responsible AI systems for art curation.

中文标题: Artographer：艺术空间探索的策展界面

中文摘要: 将作品与先前确立的作品联系起来对于创作和参与艺术至关重要，但AI界面往往模糊了这种关系，而不是帮助用户探索它们。嵌入模型为通过空间交互发现和关联艺术品提供了新的机会。我们构建了Artographer，这是一个艺术探索系统，具有可缩放的2D地图，由15,000+历史艺术品的相似性聚类嵌入构建而成。使用Artographer作为探究空间艺术品探索的工具，我们分析了20名参与者（包括9名艺术史学者）在目标驱动任务和自由探索期间如何遍历地图。我们观察到发散和收敛的探索行为（跳跃、漫游、专注、重访），并识别了空间艺术发现所体现的价值（可见性、能动性、偶然性、摩擦）。我们将空间地图置于策展界面的空间中，这些系统选择和呈现艺术品，并讨论在设计更负责任的艺术策展AI系统时，如何以多元主义和能动性为中心。

</details>


### [108] [A Visual Analytics System to Understand Behaviors of Multi Agents in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02442)
*Changhee Lee,Jeongmin Rhee,DongHwa Shin*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 开发了MARLViz可视化分析系统，用于理解和分析多智能体强化学习环境中智能体的行为和交互模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体强化学习（MARL）涉及多个智能体在复杂环境中的交互，但现有分析方法难以充分反映和解释这种复杂性，需要更好的可视化工具来理解智能体行为和交互模式。

Method: 开发了MARLViz可视化分析系统，通过可视化展示不同环境设置下智能体行为的差异，分析具有相似行为的智能体，并选择特定场景来理解智能体交互。

Result: MARLViz系统能够直观展示智能体在不同环境下的行为差异，帮助用户理解复杂的交互模式，使理解MARL中智能体策略变得更加容易。

Conclusion: MARLViz可视化分析系统有效解决了多智能体强化学习中理解和分析智能体行为及交互的挑战，为复杂MARL环境中的策略理解提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) is a branch of machine learning in which agents interact and learn optimal policies through trial and error, addressing complex scenarios where multiple agents interact and learn in the same environment at the same time. Analyzing and understanding these complex interactions is challenging, and existing analysis methods are limited in their ability to fully reflect and interpret this complexity. To address these challenges, we provide MARLViz, a visual analytics system for visualizing and analyzing the policies and interactions of agents in MARL environments. The system is designed to visually show the difference in behavior of agents under different environment settings and help users understand complex interaction patterns. In this study, we analyzed agents with similar behaviors and selected scenarios to understand the interactions of the agents, which made it easier to understand the strategies of agents in MARL.

中文标题: 用于理解强化学习中多智能体行为的可视化分析系统

中文摘要: 多智能体强化学习（MARL）是机器学习的一个分支，智能体通过试错进行交互和学习最优策略，处理多个智能体在同一环境中同时交互和学习的复杂场景。分析和理解这些复杂的交互具有挑战性，现有的分析方法在充分反映和解释这种复杂性方面存在局限性。为了解决这些挑战，我们提供了MARLViz，一个用于可视化和分析MARL环境中智能体策略和交互的可视化分析系统。该系统旨在直观展示不同环境设置下智能体行为的差异，并帮助用户理解复杂的交互模式。在本研究中，我们分析了具有相似行为的智能体并选择了场景来理解智能体的交互，这使得更容易理解MARL中智能体的策略。

### [109] [Reframing Human-Robot Interaction Through Extended Reality: Unlocking Safer, Smarter, and More Empathic Interactions with Virtual Robots and Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02569)
*Yuchong Zhang,Yong Ma,Danica Kragic*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本文提出通过扩展现实(XR)重构人机交互(HRI)，利用大型基础模型驱动的虚拟机器人作为具有认知基础和共情能力的智能体，突破物理硬件限制，实现更安全、智能和共情的交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统物理机器人受硬件限制，难以实现灵活适应、安全关键场景和深度共情交互。本文旨在探索XR与基础模型结合，创造不受物理约束、可即时实例化、适应性强且具备认知共情能力的虚拟机器人，以重塑人机交互范式。

Method: 综合XR、HRI和认知AI领域研究，提出利用多模态大型基础模型（如大语言模型、大视觉模型、视觉语言模型）为虚拟机器人提供上下文感知推理、情感敏感情境理解和长期适应能力，使其成为认知共情中介而非单纯模拟资产。

Result: 虚拟机器人能够支持安全关键场景、跨领域的社会认知共情交互，并通过XR与AI集成扩展物理能力。同时识别了包括过度信任、文化偏见、生物识别隐私、数据治理等挑战和潜在风险。

Conclusion: 提出以人为中心、伦理为基础的XR智能体研究议程，强调多层评估框架、多用户生态系统、混合虚拟-物理体现以及社会伦理设计实践，将基于基础模型的XR虚拟智能体定位为重塑未来人机交互为更高效、自适应范式的重要方向。

Abstract: This perspective reframes human-robot interaction (HRI) through extended reality (XR), arguing that virtual robots powered by large foundation models (FMs) can serve as cognitively grounded, empathic agents. Unlike physical robots, XR-native agents are unbound by hardware constraints and can be instantiated, adapted, and scaled on demand, while still affording embodiment and co-presence. We synthesize work across XR, HRI, and cognitive AI to show how such agents can support safety-critical scenarios, socially and cognitively empathic interaction across domains, and outreaching physical capabilities with XR and AI integration. We then discuss how multimodal large FMs (e.g., large language model, large vision model, and vision-language model) enable context-aware reasoning, affect-sensitive situations, and long-term adaptation, positioning virtual robots as cognitive and empathic mediators rather than mere simulation assets. At the same time, we highlight challenges and potential risks, including overtrust, cultural and representational bias, privacy concerns around biometric sensing, and data governance and transparency. The paper concludes by outlining a research agenda for human-centered, ethically grounded XR agents - emphasizing multi-layered evaluation frameworks, multi-user ecosystems, mixed virtual-physical embodiment, and societal and ethical design practices to envision XR-based virtual agents powered by FMs as reshaping future HRI into a more efficient and adaptive paradigm.

中文标题: 通过扩展现实重构人机交互：利用虚拟机器人和基础模型解锁更安全、智能和共情的交互

中文摘要: 本文从扩展现实(XR)的角度重构人机交互(HRI)，认为由大型基础模型驱动的虚拟机器人可以作为具有认知基础和共情能力的智能体。与物理机器人不同，XR原生智能体不受硬件约束，可以按需实例化、适应和扩展，同时仍能提供具身化和共在感。我们综合了XR、HRI和认知AI领域的研究，展示了此类智能体如何支持安全关键场景、跨领域的社会认知共情交互，以及通过XR与AI集成扩展物理能力。然后讨论了多模态大型基础模型（如大语言模型、大视觉模型和视觉语言模型）如何实现上下文感知推理、情感敏感情境理解和长期适应，将虚拟机器人定位为认知和共情中介而非单纯的模拟资产。同时，我们强调了挑战和潜在风险，包括过度信任、文化和表征偏见、生物识别隐私问题以及数据治理和透明度。本文最后概述了以人为中心、伦理为基础的XR智能体研究议程，强调多层评估框架、多用户生态系统、混合虚拟-物理体现以及社会伦理设计实践，展望基于基础模型的XR虚拟智能体将重塑未来HRI为更高效和自适应的范式。

### [110] [Real-Time Multimodal Data Collection Using Smartwatches and Its Visualization in Education](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.02651)
*Alvaro Becerra,Pablo Villegas,Ruth Cobos*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 本文开发了Watch-DMLT和ViSeDOPS两个工具，用于通过智能手表实时采集多模态教育数据并进行可视化分析，解决了教育环境中多模态学习分析数据采集的同步性和可扩展性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可穿戴传感器如智能手表在教育领域提供了研究认知和情感过程的新机会，但缺乏可扩展、同步和高分辨率的多模态数据采集工具，阻碍了多模态学习分析在实际教育环境中的广泛应用。

Method: 开发了两个互补工具：Watch-DMLT（用于Fitbit Sense 2智能手表的数据采集应用，支持实时多用户生理和运动信号监测）和ViSeDOPS（基于仪表板的可视化系统，用于分析口语演示期间收集的同步多模态数据）。

Result: 在涉及65名学生和最多16个智能手表的课堂部署中，成功捕获并分析了包括心率、运动、注视、视频和上下文注释在内的数据流，证明了系统在真实学习环境中支持细粒度、可扩展和可解释的多模态学习分析的可行性和实用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的系统解决了多模态学习分析在真实教育环境中的关键挑战，为教育研究提供了有效的工具，支持对学习过程中认知和情感状态的深入理解。

Abstract: Wearable sensors, such as smartwatches, have become increasingly prevalent across domains like healthcare, sports, and education, enabling continuous monitoring of physiological and behavioral data. In the context of education, these technologies offer new opportunities to study cognitive and affective processes such as engagement, attention, and performance. However, the lack of scalable, synchronized, and high-resolution tools for multimodal data acquisition continues to be a significant barrier to the widespread adoption of Multimodal Learning Analytics in real-world educational settings. This paper presents two complementary tools developed to address these challenges: Watch-DMLT, a data acquisition application for Fitbit Sense 2 smartwatches that enables real-time, multi-user monitoring of physiological and motion signals; and ViSeDOPS, a dashboard-based visualization system for analyzing synchronized multimodal data collected during oral presentations. We report on a classroom deployment involving 65 students and up to 16 smartwatches, where data streams including heart rate, motion, gaze, video, and contextual annotations were captured and analyzed. Results demonstrate the feasibility and utility of the proposed system for supporting fine-grained, scalable, and interpretable Multimodal Learning Analytics in real learning environments.

中文标题: 使用智能手表进行实时多模态数据收集及其在教育中的可视化

中文摘要: 可穿戴传感器（如智能手表）在医疗保健、体育和教育等领域日益普及，能够持续监测生理和行为数据。在教育背景下，这些技术为研究参与度、注意力和表现等认知和情感过程提供了新机会。然而，缺乏可扩展、同步和高分辨率的多模态数据采集工具仍然是多模态学习分析在实际教育环境中广泛采用的重要障碍。本文提出了两个互补工具来解决这些挑战：Watch-DMLT（用于Fitbit Sense 2智能手表的数据采集应用，支持实时多用户生理和运动信号监测）和ViSeDOPS（基于仪表板的可视化系统，用于分析口语演示期间收集的同步多模态数据）。我们报告了一个涉及65名学生和最多16个智能手表的课堂部署，其中捕获并分析了包括心率、运动、注视、视频和上下文注释在内的数据流。结果表明，所提出的系统在真实学习环境中支持细粒度、可扩展和可解释的多模态学习分析方面具有可行性和实用性。
